---STRING#48@L703---
JP:仲間は戦闘に遭遇すると自動で戦闘を開始します。[NLINE]
ただしそれが重要な戦闘の場合、開始時に[NLINE]
あなたに指示を求めてきます。[NWIN]

行動中の仲間に指示したい場合は、[NLINE]
[TRIANGLE]を押してメニューを開き、指示したい仲間へ[NLINE]
[L1]、[R1]で切り替えてコマンドを選んでください。[NWIN]

行動内容は主人公と同じように指示できます。[NLINE]
ただし、非戦闘時は移動や攻撃といったコマンド[NLINE]
は使用できないことが多いです。[NWIN]

指示の行動を終えると再度指示を求めてきますが、[NLINE]
コンフィグの[COL01]『命令終了時の思考』[COL00]をＡＵＴＯに[NLINE]
すると、再指示を求めないようにもできます。[END-FE]
System Message\\
EN:Party members automatically enter combat[NLINE]
when they encounter enemies. However, if[NLINE]
it's an important battle, they will ask for[NLINE]
instructions before the start.[NWIN]
If you want to issue an order during a[NLINE]
fight, press [TRIANGLE] to open up the menu[NLINE]
and [L1] and [R1] to switch to the party[NLINE]
member.[NWIN]
The orders you can give to the main[NLINE]
character are also available for party[NLINE]
members. However, orders such as Move[NLINE]
and Attack are often not available during[NLINE]
non-combat.[NWIN]
When the action is completed, the party member[NLINE]
will ask for further instructions. However,[NLINE]
if [COL01]"Post-Instruction Behaviour"[COL00] in the[NLINE]
Config Menu is set to AUTO, the character[NLINE]
will not ask for instructions again.[END-FE]
